### [102] [Rate-Utility Frontiers for Language Encodings: Comparing Tokens, Bytes, and Pixels Under Controlled Linguistic Content](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16117)
*Ingo Ziegler,Martin Krebs,Desmond Elliott*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过控制内容和下游能力，在13种语言和5种文字中系统比较了子词、字节和像素三种编码方式在率-效用曲线上的表现。结果表明：没有一种编码在所有任务或容量区间中占优——像素保留表面形式最优，字节在多语言同文字场景下跨语言对齐最佳，子词对主题分类支持最好。编码选择本质上是率-效用权衡，取决于任务、语言组合、容量和计算预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多在不对等约束下比较不同编码（如不同模型暴露不同语言内容），本文希望在控制内容与下游容量的前提下，公平评估子词、字节、像素三种编码对语言信息的保留能力。

Method: 使用13种语言5种文字的平行句子，通过共享瓶颈（bottleneck）并扫描宽度，绘制率-效用前沿（rate-utility frontiers），分离编码产生的输入位置数、编码后的潜在容量以及压缩后保留的任务相关信息。

Result: 无编码全面占优。像素保留表面形式最佳；字节在同文字多语言场景下跨语言对齐最佳；子词对主题分类最佳。序列长度不能单独解释表现差异。

Conclusion: 编码选择不是对子词、字节或像素的固定偏好，而是取决于任务、语言组合、容量区间和计算预算的率-效用权衡。

Abstract: Language models encode text as subword tokens, raw bytes, or rendered pixels, but these encodings are usually compared under modeling constraints that expose different amounts of linguistic content to models across different languages. We instead ask what each encoding preserves when both the content and the downstream capacity are controlled. Using verified parallel sentences across thirteen languages and five scripts, we compare tokens, bytes, and pixels through a shared bottleneck whose width is swept to trace rate-utility frontiers. This separates three quantities that are often conflated: the number of input positions an encoding creates, the latent capacity available after encoding, and the task-relevant information that survives compression. We evaluate three utilities: surface form preservation, cross-lingual sentence alignment, and topic classification. No encoding dominates across tasks or capacity regimes. Pixels preserve surface form best, bytes preserve cross-lingual alignment best, especially in same-script multilingual settings, and tokens support topic prediction best. These performances are not explained by sequence length alone. Short inputs can discard useful meaning, while long inputs can preserve information that compresses well. Choosing an encoding is therefore not a fixed preference for tokens, bytes, or pixels, but a rate-utility tradeoff that depends on the task, language mix, capacity regime, and compute budget.

</details>


### [103] [ToolSciVer: Multimodal Scientific Claim Verification with Visual Tool Augmented Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16131)
*Binglin Zhou,Peng Shi,Ryo Kamoi,Nan Zhang,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出ToolSciVer，首个为多模态科学声明验证设计的工具增强框架，通过为VLM配备三种感知视觉工具（表格行列聚焦、图表结构解析、高分辨率区域放大），并利用GRPO策略优化工具使用，在SciVer和MuSciClaims数据集上超越多种基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多模态科学声明验证中难以定位关键视觉证据、准确解读结构化科学图表（如表格、图表）以及将多模态观察整合为可靠推理。

Method: ToolSciVer为VLM配备三种类型感知的视觉工具：表格行列聚焦、图表结构解析、高分辨率区域放大；并使用GRPO（群体相对策略优化）在复合奖励（答案正确性、格式有效性、长度控制、工具使用效率、工具有效性惩罚）下训练工具使用策略。

Result: 在SciVer和MuSciClaims数据集上，对Qwen、InternVL、Gemma三个模型家族的五个VLM进行实验，ToolSciVer优于四种竞争基线方法（包括基于提示和基于RL的工具使用方法）。

Conclusion: 学得的类型感知工具使用策略对于科学声明验证是有效的，标志着该领域首个工具增强框架的成功。

Abstract: Multimodal Scientific Claim Verification (MSCV) requires models to verify scientific claims using visually grounded evidence from papers, including figures, tables, charts, and textual context. However, existing methods often fail because they struggle to locate decisive visual evidence, accurately read structured scientific visuals, and integrate multimodal observations into reliable reasoning. We introduce ToolSciVer, the first tool-augmented framework for MSCV to our knowledge. ToolSciVer equips a VLM with three type-aware visual tools, table row/column focus, chart-to-structure parsing, and high-resolution region zoom, which convert dense scientific visuals into explicit, claim-facing evidence, and trains the policy with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) under a composite reward of answer correctness, format validity, length control, tool-use efficiency, and tool-validity penalties. Experiments on SciVer and MuSciClaims datasets on five VLMs from three model families (Qwen, InternVL, Gemma) demonstrate that our method achieves superior performance compared to four competitive baselines including prompting-based and RL-based tool-use methods, highlighting the effectiveness of learned, type-aware tool use for scientific claim verification.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构建了CHRONO-RESOLUTION数据集，包含npm、PyPI和crates.io包在发布点的依赖解析信息及漏洞数据，并开源供后续研究使用。

Abstract: Dependency resolution at a specified point in time in the past can provide insight into software evolution in software ecosystems and facilitate the design of dynamic metrics (e.g., dependency freshness, dependency update rhythm). However, dependency resolution at specified points in time is not possible in major software ecosystems due to a lack of support from package management tools. The goal of this paper is to aid practitioners and researchers in analyzing the state of the ecosystem dependency graph at release points using an enriched dataset with dependency resolution at release points for npm, PyPI, and crates.io packages. In this paper, we present a methodology to construct dependency resolution at release points of packages in software ecosystems, which we enrich with vulnerability data from OSV. We apply our methodology to construct CHRONO-RESOLUTION, a dataset of dependency resolution at release points for npm, PyPI, and crates.io packages, and release it for future research.

### [105] [Two-Path Status Verification for Outbound Enterprise Messaging Pipelines: Webhook and Scheduled Polling Fallback Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15529)
*Devam Gupta*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双路径状态验证架构，用于解决企业外发消息管道中webhook回调失败导致CRM系统中消息状态永久挂起的问题。主路径通过实时webhook事件驱动更新，备选路径通过定时轮询任务查询提供商API进行状态对账，并引入幂等去重和同步失败检测机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业消息管道的投递状态回调（webhook）依赖网络可达性和端点可用性，一旦回调失败，CRM系统中的消息状态会永久停留在中间状态（如"发送中"），无法正确反映真实投递结果。单一依赖webhook的架构存在根本性的可靠性缺陷。

Method: 提出双路径状态验证架构：主路径通过实时webhook获取回调，经REST端点发布内部事件触发异步记录更新；备选路径由可配置的定时轮询任务检测挂起记录，直接查询提供商状态API进行状态对账。通过幂等upsert实现去重，并设计了同步失败检测机制和平台资源限制约束下的工程取舍。

Result: 双路径架构有效解决了webhook失败导致的状态挂起问题，备选路径作为容错兜底，确保了消息状态最终一致性。该架构已在基于多租户PaaS基础设施的生产级CRM消息系统中得到验证。

Conclusion: 仅依赖webhook的单一信道设计不可靠，必须引入主动轮询作为补偿机制。双路径架构通过异步事件驱动与定时对账的配合，在不增加同步复杂性的前提下大幅提升了消息状态追踪的鲁棒性，为类似企业级消息管道工程提供了可复用的设计模式。

Abstract: Outbound enterprise messaging pipelines face a fundamental reliability challenge: delivery status callbacks (webhooks) from messaging providers are subject to network failures, endpoint unavailability, and provider-side retry exhaustion, resulting in stale status records in the CRM system of record. A naive single-path architecture that relies exclusively on webhooks leaves a population of messages permanently in an intermediate state when callbacks fail. This paper presents a two-path status verification architecture, generalized from patterns observed in production CRM-native messaging systems built on multi-tenant platform-as-a-service infrastructure. The primary path uses a real-time webhook received by a REST endpoint, which publishes an internal event for asynchronous record update. The fallback path uses a configurable scheduled polling job that detects records still in transitional status after a configurable interval and queries the provider's status API directly to reconcile state. We describe the event-driven primary path, the scheduler-based fallback, deduplication via idempotent upsert, the sync failure detection mechanism, and the platform resource-limit considerations that shape each design decision.

</details>


### [106] [Understanding Agent-Reactive Bugs at the Model-Harness Boundary: An Empirical Study of LLM Agent Issue Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15684)
*Jingyi Chen,Songqiang Chen,Hengcheng Zhu,Jialun Cao,Jiasi Shen,Shing-Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文首次对LLM Agent中的"Agent响应型（AR）错误"进行实证研究。通过分析255个来自Codex、Gemini-CLI、LangChain和CrewAI的bug报告，构建了涵盖可观察症状和触发错误LLM行为的二维分类体系。研究发现AR错误常表现为无明确测试oracle的静默错误，LLM响应的随机性使错误复现困难。用户与开发者对修复方案存在认知偏差。研究强调了LLM Agent特有挑战，并为测试oracle设计、错误复现支持及故障定位技术提供了动机。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究简单地将Agent错误归因于模型能力不足或harness代码缺陷（如过时API、配置不匹配），但未深入分析那些只有特定LLM响应与Agent框架交互时才触发的"Agent响应型错误"。由于这类错误无法通过单独检查LLM或harness代码来理解，亟需系统性实证分析。

Method: 对255个来自Codex、Gemini-CLI、LangChain和CrewAI的bug报告进行人工分析，构建二维分类体系：纵向为可观察症状（如静默错误、异常行为等），横向为触发错误的LLM行为模式（如输出格式异常、推理错误等）。同时对比分析用户提出的修复建议与开发者实际实施的修复方案。

Result: 大量AR错误表现为无明确测试oracle的静默错误，检测困难；LLM响应的随机性导致错误难以复现；用户倾向于建议在harness层添加防护措施，而开发者常将问题归责于LLM或对用户修复方案反应迟缓。

Conclusion: AR错误是LLM Agent特有的错误类型，现有测试和调试方法难以应对。研究呼吁开发针对AR错误的测试oracle、错误复现支持和故障定位技术，并改善用户与开发者之间的沟通机制。

Abstract: LLM agents span command-line interfaces (e.g., Codex) and agent frameworks (e.g., LangChain), integrating backend LLMs with harness code that parses model outputs, controls agent loops, and manages context. Both the harness and LLM-generated responses jointly shape an agent's execution. This architecture gives rise to bugs that cannot be readily understood by inspecting either component alone, because some bugs occur only when a particular LLM response elicits an abnormal reaction from the agent. Prior empirical studies of agent bugs have largely attributed failures either to limited model capabilities or to harness-side defects, such as outdated APIs and configuration misalignment, without characterizing these AR bugs. We conduct the first empirical study focused on agent-reactive (AR) bugs. Through manual analysis of 255 bug reports from Codex, Gemini-CLI, LangChain, and CrewAI, we construct a two-axis taxonomy covering observable symptoms and the LLM behaviors that trigger them. Our findings show that many AR bugs manifest as silent errors without well-defined test oracles, which makes detection difficult. The stochasticity of LLM responses further complicates bug reproduction. We additionally examine fixes proposed by users and implemented by developers. This analysis exposes a mismatch: users frequently advocate harness-side guardrails, whereas developers may attribute the issue to the LLM or respond slowly to user-proposed fixes. These findings point to the need for mechanisms that help users and developers understand the root causes and resolutions of AR bugs. Overall, the study highlights challenges specific to LLM agents and motivates the design of test oracles, reproduction support, and fault-localization techniques for AR bugs.

</details>


### [107] [Verified LLM-Driven Synthesis for Concept Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15718)
*Alcino Cunha*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于概念（concept）和反应（reaction）的软件设计形式化语义，并利用CEGIS框架结合LLM来综合满足安全不变量的反应设计。评估表明，仅靠不变量约束不足，自然语言提示不如场景引导有效，而LLM驱动的场景启发技术有助于早期设计探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概念设计方法虽能模块化构建软件系统，但缺少形式化基础来保证安全性，且手动设计反应规则繁琐易错。作者希望通过形式化语义和自动综合来弥补这一缺口。

Method: 1) 给出概念与反应的形式化语义，支持安全不变量自动验证；2) 提出CEGIS风格的LLM驱动合成过程，生成满足不变量的反应设计；3) 利用自然语言提示和正/负场景两种方式引导合成走向用户意图；4) 提出LLM驱动的场景启发技术辅助早期设计探索。

Result: 在三个应用和十二个设计变体上评估发现：仅用不变量合成虽快但结果不一致且常不可行；场景引导比自然语言提示更一致地恢复预期设计，但最小场景可能导致过拟合；LLM驱动的场景启发在足够场景下能恢复多数变体的预期设计，但遗漏行为和非确定性使其无法全覆盖。

Conclusion: 不变量约束不足以唯一确定设计意图，场景是更有效的引导手段。LLM驱动的场景启发降低了用户编写场景的负担，但仍需改进覆盖能力。未来工作可探索更鲁棒的场景生成与用户交互策略。

Abstract: Concept Design structures software systems around concepts: user-facing, self-contained units of functionality with a focused purpose. Concepts are composed into applications using synchronization rules called reactions, which specify how actions in one concept trigger actions in others. This paper first gives a formal semantics for concepts and reactions, enabling automatic verification of safety invariants in applications developed with this methodology. It then presents a CEGIS-style, LLM-driven synthesis procedure for generating reaction designs that satisfy such invariants. Because many different designs can satisfy the same invariant, we study two ways of steering synthesis toward the user's intended design: natural-language prompts and positive/negative scenarios. We also propose an LLM-driven scenario elicitation technique to support early design exploration. In an evaluation on three applications and twelve design variants using one LLM configuration, invariant-only synthesis reached verified designs quickly but often produced inconsistent designs across runs, some of which were implausible, showing that invariants alone underconstrain the design task. Scenario-guided synthesis recovered intended designs more consistently than natural-language prompting, although minimal scenarios can lead to overfitting. LLM-driven scenario elicitation, where the user classifies proposed scenarios rather than authoring them from scratch, recovered the intended designs in most variants when enough scenarios were elicited, but missed behaviors and non-determinism prevented reliable coverage in all cases.

</details>


### [108] [GapForge: Directed Compiler Fuzzing via Coverage-Gap Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15762)
*Mingxuan Zhu,Qingyuan Liang,Junjie Chen,Zhihong Xue,Dan Hao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: GapForge是一种基于LLM的编译器测试生成技术，通过覆盖缺口分析，在GCC和LLVM上分别达到68.13%和69.11%的覆盖率，远超现有方法，并发现了12个真实编译器缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代编译器（如GCC、LLVM）代码库庞大复杂，现有测试生成技术无法充分覆盖多样化的代码区域，导致长期存在的覆盖缺口（long-tail coverage gaps）持续存在，即使是白盒技术在大规模编译器上也覆盖率有限。

Method: 三步法：1）基于覆盖率的文件评分优先处理大且覆盖不足的文件；2）对每段未覆盖代码进行路径差异分析，推断触发条件（程序结构和编译选项）；3）综合需求与历史失败提示，利用覆盖率反馈迭代生成测试程序。

Result: 在GCC 14.3.0和LLVM 19.1.0上，72小时内核心模块覆盖率分别达68.13%和69.11%，比白盒方法WhiteFox多覆盖24,736行（GCC）和19,798行（LLVM），发现12个真实缺陷（5个GCC，7个LLVM），包括8个崩溃和4个误编译。

Conclusion: GapForge通过将覆盖缺口作为显式区域级目标，结合路径分析和LLM生成，有效提升了编译器边缘区域的测试覆盖率，各组件均对其性能有贡献。

Abstract: Modern compiler codebases (e.g., GCC and LLVM) are large and complex, making comprehensive coverage across diverse code regions highly challenging. Most existing test generation techniques ignore characteristics of the target code, producing test programs that exercise only a limited subset of it. Consequently, substantial compiler regions remain insufficiently tested, leaving persistent long-tail coverage gaps that survive across releases. Even existing white-box techniques achieve limited coverage on large-scale compilers. To improve compiler coverage, especially for hard-to-reach edge regions, we present GapForge, a targeted LLM-based test generation technique that reasons about coverage gaps. Unlike program-driven techniques that generate diverse inputs without modeling which regions they exercise, and unlike whole-file summarization that yields coarse guidance, GapForge treats coverage gaps as explicit region-level targets in three steps. First, it prioritizes files via coverage-driven scoring that favors large, undercovered files. Second, it pairs each uncovered line span with its enclosing covered context and performs path-difference analysis to infer fine-grained triggering requirements: the program structures and compilation options needed to reach the uncovered region. Third, it synthesizes prompts from these requirements and previously failed prompts, using coverage feedback to guide next-round selection. On GCC 14.3.0 and LLVM 19.1.0, GapForge significantly outperforms eight state-of-the-art techniques. Within 72 hours, it achieves 68.13% and 69.11% coverage on core compiler modules in GCC and LLVM, surpassing the white-box technique WhiteFox by 24,736 and 19,798 additional lines, respectively. Moreover, GapForge discovers 12 real-world compiler failures (5 in GCC, 7 in LLVM), including 8 crashes and 4 miscompilations, with each component contributing to its performance.

</details>


### [109] [Making Agent-Mediated Contributions Governable: A Project-Level Governance Manifest for Open-Source AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15769)
*Jinjin Gao,Luyang Li,Shufen Guo,Ligang He,Xiaoning Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文针对生成式AI和编码代理加剧的开源软件治理张力问题，提出了“项目侧可治理性基础设施”的理论概念，设计了代理治理清单（AGM）作为边界资源与双向治理契约。对50个GitHub仓库的审计发现缺乏全局治理安排；15人参与的评审侧实验显示AGM显著提升风险标签恢复率（37/38 vs 15/37）和评审支持感知（6.14 vs 3.27）；15人参与的贡献者侧可行性检验中45项任务均正确表达核心治理状态。最终提出了可读性、可追溯性、可治理性三层框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI和编码代理极大加速了贡献生成，但维护者评估风险、证据和问责的能力未能同步提升，导致开源治理张力加剧。现有方案侧重提升代理可读性和可追溯性，但缺乏将贡献特定风险、证据、问责和审核关口状态组织起来的项目侧治理基础设施。

Method: 对50个GitHub仓库进行诊断审计；设计代理治理清单（AGM）作为仓库托管的边界资源与双向治理契约；开展15人参与的评审侧控制实验和15人参与的贡献者侧可行性检验。

Result: 审计发现存在普遍治理工件、可观察的代理可读性及碎片化AI治理线索，但缺乏全局性协调安排。评审侧实验中，AGM支持的材料将精确风险标签恢复率从15/37提升至37/38，评审支持感知从3.27提升至6.14（1-7量表）。贡献者侧检验中所有45项任务最终包均正确表达核心治理状态，41项通过严格结构验证。

Conclusion: 提出了可读性、可追溯性、可治理性三层框架，将代理介导的贡献理论化为可治理的边界对象，推进了合规赋能型数字创新治理，同时维护了维护者的决策权威。

Abstract: Generative AI and coding agents are intensifying a central governance tension in open-source software (OSS): they scale contribution generation faster than maintainers can assess risk, evidence, and accountability. Existing responses improve agent-readability and traceability, but project rules must also organize contribution-specific risk, evidence, accountability, and review-gate states. We theorize this organizational arrangement as project-side governability infrastructure. A diagnostic audit of 50 GitHub repositories finds widespread general governance artifacts, observable agent-readability, and fragmented AI-governance cues, but no project-wide arrangement that coordinates shared rules, preparation obligations, verification rights, and maintainer decision authority across AI-mediated contribution workflows. We develop the Agent Governance Manifest (AGM) as a repository-hosted boundary resource and bidirectional governance contract linking contributor-side evidence preparation with maintainer-side verification. In a controlled reviewer-side evaluation with 15 participants and 75 task-level outputs, AGM-supported materials improved exact risk-label recovery (37/38 vs. 15/37) and perceived review support (6.14 vs. 3.27 on a 1-7 scale). In a contributor-side feasibility check, 15 participants completed 45 tasks; all final packages represented the core governance state correctly, and 41 passed strict structural validation. The study develops a three-layer framework of agent-readability, traceability, and governability, theorizes agent-mediated contributions as governable boundary objects, and advances compliance-enabling digital innovation governance while preserving maintainer decision authority.

</details>


### [110] [READU: Inconsistency-Driven Just-in-Time Detection and Repair of README Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15780)
*Doehyun Baek,Kilian Krampf,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出 READU，一种基于不一致性检测的 README 文档错误（README bugs）的即时检测与自动修复技术，通过内部一致性（与源代码对比）和外部一致性（与外部依赖对比）检查，在六个流行仓库上达到 75% 精度，并能自动合成补丁修复 217 个错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仓库级文档（如 README）常存在错误，导致用户运行时出错或浪费时间调试。由于文档混合了代码与自然语言，与源代码之间的关联松散，且发现错误后仍需开发者手动修复，因此亟需一种自动化检测与修复技术。

Method: READU 的核心思路是 README 错误常表现为文档与内部事实（源代码）或外部事实（外部依赖）之间的不一致。方法包括：高召回率的提交过滤器；并行运行内部一致性检查器（与源代码对比）和外部一致性检查器（与外部依赖对比）；使用告警裁判去除误报；自动合成文档补丁。

Result: 在 6,000 个来自 Linux、Spring Boot 等六个流行仓库的近期提交上，READU 检测出 244 个真阳性，精度达 75%，平均每次提交耗时不到 1 分钟，成本低于 $0.01。其中 217 个真阳性被正确修复。已报告 66 个发现的 README 错误，44 个已确认，26 个已修复。

Conclusion: READU 能够高效、低成本地自动检测和修复 README 文档中的不一致性错误，具有良好的实用价值；实验表明该方法在真实仓库中有效，并已获得开发者社区的积极反馈。

Abstract: Repository-level documentation, such as READMEs, is often the first point of contact between users and a repository. When this documentation is incorrect, users may encounter runtime errors or waste their time debugging. We call such mistakes in repository-level documentation README bugs. Addressing README bugs is challenging because documentation mixes prose with code, its connection to the source of truth is loose, and finding a bug still leaves developers to craft a repair. This paper presents READU, an inconsistency-driven technique for just-in-time detection and repair of README bugs. The key insight behind READU is that README bugs often manifest as inconsistencies between documentation and another source of truth: either repository-internal facts, such as source code, or repository-external facts, such as external dependencies. READU applies a high-recall commit filter, runs internal and external consistency checkers in parallel, uses an alert judge to remove false positives, and automatically synthesizes documentation patches. On 6,000 recent commits from six popular repositories including Linux and Spring Boot, READU detects 244 true positives with 75% precision, while consuming less than $0.01 and less than one minute per commit, on average. Of these true positives, READU correctly repairs 217. We report 66 found README bugs, of which (so far) 44 are confirmed and 26 are fixed.

</details>


### [111] [In the Driver's Seat: A Multi-Company Study on the Reality of Autonomous Driving System Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15820)
*Qunying Song,Yuan Gao,Johannes Betz,Dietmar Pfahl,Mohammad Reza Mousavi,Federica Sarro*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对来自6个国家9家公司的自动驾驶系统（ADS）测试专家进行访谈研究，系统总结了当前ADS测试的工业实践、挑战与未来趋势，并提出了一个以证据为中心的闭环测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自动驾驶系统在实际场景中快速部署，缺乏成熟的测试标准（场景选择、性能评估、验收标准等），亟需系统了解工业界当前的测试实践与面临的挑战。

Method: 采用访谈研究方法，对来自6个国家9家公司的ADS开发与测试专家进行半结构化访谈，并通过主题分析法（Thematic Analysis）对访谈数据进行归纳总结。

Result: 当前ADS测试主要采用基于场景和X-in-the-loop方法，面临场景真实性、场景覆盖率、仿真保真度和验收标准等主要挑战；参与者提出了AI、世界模型和端到端方法等潜在解决方案，并认为未来测试将更加自动化、数据驱动和透明化。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了工业视角下ADS测试的综合概览，提出了以证据为中心的闭环测试框架，为ADS测试提供了可操作的指导，并为未来研究和实践指明了方向。

Abstract: Autonomous driving systems (ADS) are rapidly advancing and increasingly deployed in real-world applications. This creates growing demands for effective testing to ensure system functionality and safety. However, ADS testing remains complex and lacks well-established standards for scenario selection, performance evaluation, and acceptance criteria. To better understand current ADS testing practices and challenges, we conducted an interview study with experts working on ADS development and testing in nine companies from six different countries. Through thematic analysis, we synthesized industrial testing practices, challenges, potential solutions, future trends, and proposed an evidence-centered closed-loop testing framework for ADS testing. Our findings show that current practices primarily focus on scenario-based and X-in-the-loop testing approaches, supported by diverse tools, metrics, benchmarks, and testing strategies. The participants highlighted major challenges related to scenario realism, scenario coverage, simulation fidelity, and acceptance criteria, while also discussing potential solutions such as the use of AI, world models, and end-to-end approaches. Furthermore, participants envisioned future ADS testing to become more automated, data-driven, and transparent across the industry. Overall, this study provides a comprehensive industry-grounded overview of ADS testing, proposes an evidence-centered closed-loop testing framework to provide actionable guidance for ADS testing, and outlines important directions for future research and practice.

</details>


### [112] [Agentic Synthesis against Counterexample-Supplemented Sketches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15854)
*Muness Castle,Eric Rubeck*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对代码智能体的"反例补充草图"方法，通过人类交互与代码智能体协同，在发现失败案例时人工确认正确行为后，智能体自动修正代码草图并重建代码。在CatSynth实验中，该方法相比回放所有案例的方式，减少了开发调用次数和代码修改量，同时保持了更好的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码智能体修复失败示例时，往往会丢失导致失败的领域规则，导致后续迭代重复同样的错误。现有方法缺乏机制来确保修复过程中学到的策略被正确保留。

Method: 人类提供部分代码草图，代码智能体生成初始实现；当出现失败案例时，操作员显式确认正确的行为和规则，智能体根据反例修正草图并修复/重新生成相关代码；保留完整源数据，使用回归测试集把关每次修订，并定期进行干净重建测试。

Result: 在CatSynth实验中，14个冻结候选案例中有8个成为反例；从演化后的草图重建通过了19/21个保留案例（初始草图为15/21）；保留代码方式仅需9次开发调用和719行累计产物变更（回放所有案例需15次和2394行），通过了18/21个保留案例。

Conclusion: 演化后的草图有效承载了经过审查的策略，保留代码减少了返工量；但受限于单一模型和单次揭示顺序，不能证明方法的普遍优越性或超越编码检查的正确性。

Abstract: Coding agents can fix a failing example without preserving the domain rule that made it fail, so later generations can repeat the same plausible mistake. We present agentic synthesis against counterexample-supplemented sketches, a repository-native method for systems whose governing policy is discovered during implementation. A human starts with a partial, code-shaped sketch, and a coding agent generates the first implementation. When a concrete failure exposes missing or mistaken policy, an operator explicitly approves the corrected behavior and rule. The agent then revises the sketch and repairs or regenerates code and prompt surfaces for that one counterexample. The full archive preserves provenance; a selected regression set gates each revision before the next candidate is revealed; and periodic clean regeneration tests whether the evolved sketch, rather than prompt history or accumulated examples, carries the learned policy.
  We demonstrate the method with CatSynth, a synthetic browser application and captured coding-agent experiment. In one open-world run with GPT-5.4-mini, 8 of 14 frozen candidate cases became counterexamples. The rebuild controls inherited that promotion schedule, and all three paths passed the 8 accepted cases. Rebuilding from the evolved sketch passed 19 of 21 withheld cases, compared with 15 of 21 when rebuilding from the initial sketch and replaying all accepted examples. Retaining code across counterexamples required 9 Developer calls and 719 lines of cumulative artifact churn, versus 15 calls and 2,394 lines for replay-all, and passed 18 of 21 withheld cases. These results provide inspectable evidence that the evolved sketch carried reviewed policy and that retaining code reduced rework in this run; with one model and one reveal order, they do not establish general superiority or correctness beyond the encoded checks.

</details>


### [113] [Trans-Domain Digital Twin: Conceptual Foundations, Architecture, and Research Outlook](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15908)
*Mansoorali Amiri*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出跨域数字孪生（Trans-Domain Digital Twin）框架，通过对齐共享状态、耦合数据/模型/误差/目标/控制、异构时序协调、联合决策与反馈自适应，在复合/联邦数字孪生系统连续统上实现跨异构领域的形式化操作连接。该框架包括七层概念架构、编排核心、最小合规条件、通用操作形式、快-中-慢渐进循环、单幕离线训练与有界在线自适应机制，并定义了成熟度模型、参考部署架构、运行时安全与模型生命周期管理要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有跨域数字孪生方法聚焦于比较、复用、语义映射、标准化和互操作性，但未内在地要求领域间状态、误差、目标、约束、决策和控制的操作性连接，缺乏形式化的跨域操作闭环。

Method: 提出跨域数字孪生框架，包含：七层概念架构、跨域编排核心、最小合规条件、通用操作形式化描述、渐进式快-中-慢循环、单幕离线训练+有界在线自适应机制，以及成熟度模型、参考部署架构、运行时安全与生命周期管理。

Result: 提供了概念验证与评估准则、成熟度模型、可映射至数字孪生/模型交换/分布式仿真/智能传感器等标准，但正式合规性与操作有效性需通过独立基准、不确定性量化、消融测试和现场验证。

Conclusion: 跨域数字孪生作为复合/联邦数字孪生系统中的新操作范式，有望弥合异构领域间的操作鸿沟，但其有效性仍需严格的实证评估与标准化合规检验。

Abstract: Complex systems comprise heterogeneous domains whose states, uncertainties, risks, and control consequences can cross domain boundaries. Existing cross-domain digital twin approaches broadly focus on comparison, reuse, semantic mapping, standardization, and interoperability, but do not inherently require operational connections among domain states, errors, objectives, constraints, decisions, and controls. This article proposes the trans-domain digital twin as an operational formulation along the continuum of Composite/Federated Digital Twin Systems. This approach connects heterogeneous domain twins through an aligned shared state, explicit coupling of data, models, states, errors, objectives, and controls, heterogeneous temporal coordination, joint decision-making, and feedback-based adaptation. The proposed framework presents a seven-layer conceptual architecture, a trans-domain orchestration core, minimum compliance conditions, a general operational formalism, progressive fast-meso-slow loops, and a single-episode offline training mechanism linked to bounded online adaptation. It also describes conceptual validation and evaluation criteria, a maturity model, a reference deployment architecture, and requirements for runtime safety, provenance, versioning, and model lifecycle management. The framework is conceptually mappable to standards for digital twins, model exchange, distributed simulation, and smart transducers; however, its formal compliance and operational effectiveness must be examined through independent benchmarks, uncertainty quantification, ablation testing, and field validation.

</details>


### [114] [TARS: A Theory-of-Mind Agent for Personalized In-IDE Code Comprehension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15948)
*Leopoldo Todisco,Antonio Della Porta,Stefano Lambiase,Fabio Palomba*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TARS是一个集成在VS Code中的LLM代理，通过轻量级心智理论模型分析开发者画像，结合RAG技术提供个性化代码解释，实验表明使用TARS的开发者任务完成速度提高26%，认知负荷更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码理解是软件工程中最耗时的任务之一，现有基于LLM的助手忽略用户差异、依赖复制粘贴式工作流，缺乏个性化适应能力。

Method: 构建TARS代理，集成到VS Code中；采用轻量级心智理论范式分析开发者的专业知识、角色和风格偏好；利用RAG技术从项目文档中检索信息，生成与代码直接锚定的自适应解释。

Result: 18名参与者的受控实验表明：使用TARS的参与者任务完成速度快26%，认知负荷更低，且认为解释能根据其个人资料进行有意义的调整。

Conclusion: 基于心智理论的个性化代码解释代理能有效提升代码理解效率、降低认知负荷，为LLM辅助编程提供了一种更贴合开发者需求的交互范式。

Abstract: Code comprehension is one of the most time-consuming tasks in software engineering, yet most LLM-based assistants produce explanations that ignore who is asking and force developers into a disruptive copy-paste workflow. We present TARS, an LLM-powered agent integrated into Visual Studio Code that supports program comprehension through autonomous explanations anchored directly to the code under analysis. Built around a lightweight Theory of Mind paradigm, TARS profiles a developer's expertise, role, and stylistic preferences, then adapts the depth and tone of its explanations accordingly, grounding them in project documentation via Retrieval-Augmented Generation. To evaluate TARS, we conducted a controlled experiment with 18 participants on non-trivial Java snippets. Participants using TARS completed tasks 26\% faster, reported lower cognitive load, and found the explanations meaningfully adapted to their profiles.

### [115] [DiffTestGen: Change-Directed LLM-Based Testing for Exposing Behavioral Differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16024)
*Huimin Hu,Cristian Cadar,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DiffTestGen是一种基于LLM的差异测试方法，通过静态调用图分析、项目文档和联合覆盖率指标，有效暴露代码变更前后的行为差异，在463个PR中达到78.2%的差异暴露率和90.7%的联合覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件演化过程中需要确保行为变更符合开发者意图，现有方法无法有效触发许多代码变更的行为差异。

Method: 利用静态调用图分析和项目文档识别有效测试入口点，引导LLM到达变更代码；通过迭代优化联合覆盖率指标（新旧版本修改代码的覆盖率组合），为LLM提供针对性覆盖率反馈。

Result: 在463个PR上，暴露78.2%的行为差异，平均联合覆盖率90.7%；相比基线多暴露99个PR，代码覆盖率分别提升12.5%和15.6个百分点；与Testora结合可检测到现有方法遗漏的回归缺陷。

Conclusion: DiffTestGen有效提升了变更导向的差分测试能力，能够发现更多行为差异和回归缺陷，在软件演化验证中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: As software evolves over time, it is important to ensure that any behavioral changes occur as intended by developers. A promising approach for this goal is to generate tests that expose behavioral differences between the old and new versions of a program. However, current approaches fail to trigger behavioral differences for many code changes. This paper presents~DiffTestGen, a novel change-directed, LLM-based differential testing approach specifically designed to expose behavioral differences introduced by a code change. The approach is enabled by two key contributions: First, DiffTestGen leverages static call graph analysis and project documentation to identify valid entry points for test generation and to guide the LLM toward reaching the changed code. Second, DiffTestGen iteratively improves our newly introduced union coverage metric, which combines coverage of modified code in the old and the new version, by providing targeted coverage feedback to the LLM. We evaluate DiffTestGen on two datasets comprising a total of 463 PRs. DiffTestGen exposes behavioral differences in 78.2% of the PRs while achieving an average union coverage of 90.7%. Compared with the baselines, DiffTestGen exposes 99 more PRs overall and increases code coverage by 12.5% and 15.6% percentage points, respectively. By integrating DiffTestGen with the Testora regression detector, we show that the identified behavioral differences can be used to detect regression bugs missed by the best existing approaches.

</details>


### [116] [What Does It Take to Research with AI? A Rapid Review of Competencies to Train LLM-Literate Researchers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16083)
*Danilo Monteiro Ribeiro,Ronnie de Souza Santos,Rodrigo Siqueira,Breno Andrade,Rafael Batista Duarte,Gilberto Hida,Julia Alencar,Gustavo Pinto*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对194篇文献的系统综述，识别出研究人员和研究生在使用大语言模型进行科研时所需的8项核心能力，其中领域专业知识与对AI输出的监督最为关键，提示培养科研人员使用LLM需要超越技术培训，整合认知、伦理和方法论素养。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在科研领域日益普及，但科研人员和研究生需要具备哪些能力才能批判性、负责任地使用这些工具，目前尚缺乏系统性的梳理和研究。

Method: 采用快速综述方法，从Elicit和Google Scholar检索2022-2025年间194篇文章，经独立双人筛选后对40篇进行能力提取和主题分析（Gwet AC1: 0.76-0.83）。

Result: 识别出8项能力，按出现频次排序：领域专业知识与AI输出监督(n=123)、元认知与AI使用决策(n=55)、伦理与学术诚信(n=53)、面向研究的提示工程(n=38)、AI使用的可重复性(n=29)、AI素养与技术知识(n=16)等。

Conclusion: 培养科研人员使用LLM需要超越纯技术培训，构建以人类对知识产出负责为核心的认知、伦理和方法论综合能力体系，对研究生课程设计和AI素养计划有直接指导意义。

Abstract: The growing adoption of Large Language Models in scientific research has created a need to understand what competencies researchers and graduate students require to use these tools critically and responsibly. This rapid review analyzed 194 articles retrieved from Elicit and Google Scholar (2022 to 2025), from which 40 were selected for competency extraction and thematic analysis following independent dual screening (Gwet AC1: 0.76 to 0.83). Eight competencies were identified. The most prevalent was domain expertise and oversight of AI outputs (n = 123), encompassing subject matter mastery, systematic skepticism, source verification, and researcher accountability. Other key competencies include metacognition and decision making about AI use (n = 55), ethics and academic integrity (n = 53), prompt engineering for research (n = 38), and reproducibility of AI use (n = 29). AI literacy and technical knowledge (n = 16) was explicitly identified as a risk factor when absent, with domain expertise treated as a prerequisite for meaningful critical evaluation. The findings suggest that preparing researchers to use LLMs goes beyond technical instruction, requiring an integrated set of epistemic, ethical, and methodological competencies centered on human accountability for the knowledge produced. These results have direct implications for the design of graduate programs and AI literacy initiatives.

</details>


### [117] [Comparison of Energy System Optimization Software and Evaluation of Selected Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16121)
*Pedro Caixeta,David Gawron,Hüseyin K. Çakmak,Haozhen Cheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文评估了五种能源系统优化软件（REMix、MTRESS、COMANDO、OEMOF、HOMER PRO）的适用场景，发现REMix适合投资路径优化，COMANDO擅长处理非标准组件，OEMOF是标准优化问题的最佳开源工具，HOMER PRO适合快速综合优化且编程经验有限的用户，而MTRESS因信息不足未能完成分析。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过广泛文献综述、文档、教程和示例模型分析，制定比较标准，对五种预选软件工具进行系统评估。

Result: REMix最适合投资路径优化；COMANDO擅长非标准组件系统；OEMOF是标准优化问题的最佳开源工具；HOMER PRO面向追求快速综合优化且编程经验少的用户；MTRESS因信息不足未完成分析。

Conclusion: 不同能源系统优化软件各有侧重和适用场景，用户应根据具体需求（如优化目标、组件特殊性和编程经验）选择合适的工具。

Abstract: Optimizing energy systems is a crucial step toward achieving a carbon-neutral future, with software tools playing a major role in the process. However, selecting the most suitable tool for specific optimization challenges can be complex, given the diverse objectives and requirements of various energy systems. In this study, we aim to address this issue by evaluating five preselected software tools-REMix, MTRESS, COMANDO, OEMOF, and HOMER PRO-to identify the scenarios for which they are most suitable. To achieve this, we conducted an extensive review of literature, documentation, tutorials, and example models, and developed a set of comparison criteria that were subsequently used to evaluate these tools. Our analysis suggests that REMix is particularly effective for scenarios where investment path optimization is required. COMANDO excels in systems with atypical components. OEMOF is the best-suited open-source tool for standard optimization problems. HOMER PRO is recommended for users seeking rapid synthesis optimization, especially those with limited programming experience. Due to difficulties in obtaining sufficient information on MTRESS, we were unable to complete the analysis for this tool.

</details>

### [118] [Fair Allocation of Divisible Goods under Non-Linear Valuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15613)
*Haris Aziz,Zixu He,Xinhang Lu,Kaiyang Zhou*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性估值下可分同质商品的公平分配问题。针对最大化份额（MMS）和 envy-freeness（EF）两种公平性属性，提出了关键算法和复杂度结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统公平分配研究多假设线性估值，但现实中代理人对商品的边际效用可能非线性。本文旨在填补非线性估值下公平分配的理论空白。

Method: 针对MMS：设计算法实现 $\frac{1}{2n-1}$-MMS 近似保证；针对EF：证明存在性和帕累托最优分配的判定问题是NP难的，并针对单商品情形提出多项式时间算法。

Result: MMS方面：$\frac{1}{2n-1}$-MMS 算法几乎最优（不可能超过 $1/n$）；$n \leq 3$ 时 $1/n$ 紧。EF方面：NP难判存在性；单商品情形可多项式时间求解。

Conclusion: 非线性估值下的公平分配存在理论界限和计算复杂度障碍，但特殊情形（如小规模或单商品）可有效求解。

Abstract: We study the problem of dividing homogeneous divisible goods among agents with non-linear valuations. Specifically, the value that an agent gains from a given good depends only on the amount of the good they receive, and is not necessarily linear with respect to the amount. For instance, under one-breakpoint piecewise-constant valuations, each agent specifies a threshold for each good such that this agent receives utility zero (resp., full utility of the good) when getting an amount below (resp., at least) the threshold. Given non-linear valuations that are additive across the goods, we focus on designing fair allocation algorithms and consider two well-known fairness properties: the maximin share (MMS) guarantee and envy-freeness (EF). For MMS, we devise an algorithm which always produces a $\frac{1}{2n-1}$-MMS allocation for $n$ agents with arbitrary non-decreasing valuations. It is worth noting that this algorithmic result is almost tight as we give an impossibility of guaranteeing more than $1/n$ approximation to MMS, even when agents have one-breakpoint piecewise-constant valuations. For $n \leq 3$ agents, we show the ratio $1/n$ is tight. Regarding envy-freeness, we show it is NP-hard to check the existence of an EF and Pareto optimal (PO) allocation for $n$ agents and at least three goods, even when agents have one-breakpoint piecewise-constant valuations. We complement the hardness result by considering the case with a single divisible good, and devising a polynomial-time algorithm to check whether an EF and PO allocation exists or not for agents with piecewise-linear valuations.

</details>

# cs.NE [[Back]](#toc)

### [119] [Evolutionary Algorithm-Guided LLMs for Physics-Informed Neural Network Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15560)
*Xu Yang,Mingyang Yu,Jing Xu,Keqian Li*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 提出了一种闭环进化算法，利用大语言模型（LLM）自动生成并优化物理信息神经网络（PINN）的配置，通过多代进化搜索找到最优架构和超参数组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PINN对架构、激活函数、损失权重等多种设计选择高度敏感，而现有LLM方法仅提供独立推荐，无法积累以往训练经验，缺乏迭代优化机制。

Method: 设计闭环进化算法，维护评估过的种群和谱系，执行父本条件变异和交叉，保留精英和多样性解，剔除重复，将成功/失败经验转化为下一代LLM的上下文，在精确优化步数预算下直接执行每个配置。

Result: 在一维多尺度波动方程上，两轮独立10代进化训练了60个PINN共60万优化步，最优配置均出现在最后一代，均方误差相比初始种群分别降低了2.97%和95.38%。

Conclusion: 进化算法引导的LLM方法在可控PDE上实现了PINN设计的可行性，为更广泛、物理感知的评估提供了动机。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) are unusually sensitive to interacting choices of architecture, activation, loss weighting, collocation, optimization, and constraint enforcement. Large language models (LLMs) can propose these choices, but independent recommendations do not accumulate experience from previously trained PINNs. We propose a closed-loop evolutionary algorithm that guides an LLM to generate complete, executable PINN configurations across generations, using measured training outcomes to determine subsequent search decisions. The algorithm maintains an evaluated population and lineage, applies parent-conditioned mutation and crossover, preserves elite and diverse solutions, rejects effective duplicates, and converts parent-relative successes and failures into the next-generation context supplied to the LLM. Every proposed configuration is executed directly under an exact optimizer-step budget. On a one-dimensional multiscale wave equation, two independent ten-generation runs trained 60 PINNs for 600,000 optimizer steps. In both runs, the best configuration appeared in the final generation, with best mean-squared error reduced by 2.97\% and 95.38\% relative to the initial population. The stronger run validated residual connections and increased depth on separate branches, combined them in a later generation, and then refined width and collocation density. It also revealed that low solution error can coexist with a high PDE residual. These results demonstrate the feasibility of evolutionary-algorithm-guided LLMs for PINN design on a controlled PDE while motivating broader, physics-aware evaluation.

### [120] [Transient State Reorganization and Cell Differentiation in the Developmental Dynamics of Growing Neural Cellular Automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15726)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 追踪完整发育轨迹；进行通道级分析、细胞状态空间的几何分析；对细胞ε-邻域网络执行社区检测以提取离散细胞类型。

Abstract: Growing Neural Cellular Automata (GNCA) develop complex morphologies from a single seed cell through shared local rules, yet the internal dynamics of this process remain poorly understood. To investigate how GNCA grows, the full developmental trajectory of trained GNCA models was traced. The trajectory of cell state development revealed that morphological convergence often proceeds non-monotonically through transient intermediate configurations. In addition, channel-wise analysis showed that the hidden channels self-organize into modular groups in parallel with the visible form. Furthermore, geometric analysis of the cell state space indicated that cell states diversify within a low-dimensional, smooth manifold. To examine cell development in more detail, community detection on an $ε$-neighbour network of cells was conducted. This analysis successfully extracted discrete cell types from this continuous space, and identified transient cell-type communities during early development and stable, finer-grained types corresponding to spatially coherent regions of the mature morphology. The temporal coordination of these phenomena across multiple independent measures indicates that the developmental process of GNCA is a reorganization of transient states rather than incremental refinement.

Abstract: Multimodal video systems often expose clip-level scores while hiding the local temporal failure that makes a video inconsistent. A formula library specifies speech-speaker agreement, audio-visual event agreement, subtitle-video agreement, scene continuity, and edit-induced temporal shock. A certificate records the trace hash, formula identifier, verdict, violating indices, defect score, first counterexample window, execution engine, and certificate hash. The certificate is not a proof that a detector is correct; it is a reproducible witness that the finite-trace checker can independently reconstruct once the atom trace is fixed. The artifact decodes real MP4 video, extracts CLIP visual atoms, extracts AST audio atoms, runs dense counterfactual perturbation sweeps, emits CSV traces and JSON certificates, and renders manuscript figures from those files.

Abstract: We present AV-JEPA, an elegant multimodal extension of LeJEPA to audio-visual self-supervised learning. Using an early-fusion Vision Transformer and modality dropout as masking, the model is trained to align the embeddings of global and per-modality local views, while the SIGReg objective encourages a theoretically optimal distribution. This achieves cross-modal alignment in the latent space, resulting in a remarkably clean architecture with no decoder, EMA teacher, complex multi-term losses, or contrastive negatives. The proposed AV-JEPA backbone delivers competitive classification performance on VGGSound (57.1% top-1) and AudioSet (32.7 mAP) and supports zero-shot audio-video retrieval out of the box.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统指令微调数据集收集方法与模型评估分离，无法针对性改进模型弱点，缺乏闭环迭代机制。

Method: 1) 构建闭环系统，每轮迭代先分析模型弱点，再生成增量数据集；2) 自适应坏例采样模块分析基准测试结果，灵活调整数据生成；3) 利用GPT-4结合代表性上下文示例生成高质量数据。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose MLLM-DataEngine, a novel closed-loop system that bridges data generation, model training, and evaluation. Within each loop iteration, the MLLM-DataEngine first analyzes the weakness of the model based on the evaluation results, then generates a proper incremental dataset for the next training iteration, and enhances the model capability iteratively. Compared with previous instruction fine-tuning dataset collection methods which are separate from the benchmarking, MLLM-DataEngine shows better targeting and can improve MLLMs's capabilities more effectively. Firstly, we propose an Adaptive Bad-case Sampling module, which can effectively analyze model weakness based on the benchmarking results and adjust the generation of incremental datasets flexibly. Secondly, in order to ensure high-quality data for specific capability types, the most representative in-context examples and abundant information are provided to GPT-4, which helps GPT-4 fully comprehend the model's weakness and further guarantees high-quality generated data. Through extensive experiments, we find MLLM-DataEngine could boost the MLLMs capability in a targeted and automatic manner without human participants. ### [124] [SPEED: One-Step Pixel Diffusion for High-quality Video Frame Interpolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15585)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Despite the success of diffusion models in Video Frame Interpolation (VFI), existing methods still suffer from two critical limitations. First, latent diffusion inevitably loses fine-grained details when reconstructing images from latent representations back to the pixel space. Second, multi-step sampling incurs prohibitive memory consumption and inference latency. To address these issues, we propose SPEED, a one-step pixel diffusion framework for high-quality VFI. Specifically, SPEED employs a progressive multi-stage architecture with dynamic patch scaling to effectively learn multi-scale motion, structural, and appearance representations. Furthermore, we propose a novel Noise-Update-Only Attention mechanism to prevent semantic degradation of the clean condition frames while reducing the computational overhead by nearly 50%. Besides, we introduce a Drift-aware Timestep Sampling strategy coupled with a tailored training objective to directly predict images in the pixel space, enabling one-step inference without compromising the quality of the generated frames. Extensive experiments show that SPEED achieves state-of-the-art performance. On SNU-FILM, SPEED reduces LPIPS by 8.8% while delivering 63.3% faster inference and 10.6% lower memory usage. On challenging 4K benchmarks, it further surpasses prior methods by up to 51.5% in LPIPS.

Abstract: Efficient representation learning is essential for optimal information storage and classification. However, it is frequently overlooked in artificial neural networks (ANNs). We analyze our previously developed biologically inspired learning rule using information-theoretic concepts, evaluating its efficiency on the MNIST classification task. The proposed rule, which emulates the brain's structural plasticity, naturally prevents overparameterization by optimizing synaptic usage and retaining only the essential number of synapses. Furthermore, it outperforms backpropagation (BP) in terms of efficiency and storage capacity. It also eliminates the need for pre-optimization of network architecture, enhances adaptability, and reflects the brain's ability to reserve 'space' for new memories. This approach advances scalable and energy-efficient AI and provides a promising framework for developing brain-inspired models that optimize resource allocation and adaptability.

### [126] [Constrained Hebbian Learning Supports Efficient Representational Allocation under Structural Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16027)
*Patrick Inoue,Florian Röhrbein,Andreas Knoblauch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了兴奋性竞争Hebbian规则在生物约束下是否比反向传播等算法能更高效地分配突触资源，发现Hebbian学习在保持相近功能性能的同时，能以更低的信息成本实现表征压缩，支持将其视为突触资源分配机制而非单纯的分类精度优化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物神经系统面临突触维护成本高和连接性有限的约束，这些约束倾向于选择能压缩行为相关信息至低冗余模式的神经编码。作者希望检验Hebbian规则是否能在此类约束下支持突触资源分配，并探索其是否比参考学习规则处于更优的成本-性能区间。

Method: 使用基于变分信息瓶颈的互信息度量来量化表征成本；在三个视听基准数据集（AVE、Kinetics-Sounds、VGGSound100）上固定视听嵌入，隔离下游关联可塑性；在匹配稀疏性和架构约束下，将Hebbian学习与密集差异目标传播（DDTP）和反向传播（BP）进行比较。

Result: Hebbian学习在主要压缩比较中实现了比稀疏BP和DDTP更低的CTI（任务信息成本），其CTI值与浅层非负权重BP相当。Hebbian学习改变了任务相关信息与表征成本之间的权衡，在多个设置中以可比的功能性能实现了更低的CTI，尽管在某些数据集上精度略有下降。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明存在成本-性能权衡而非统一的精度提升。在给定任务相关信息水平下，Hebbian表征在保持功能性能的同时保留了更少的输入信息。这些发现支持将Hebbian学习解释为一种突触资源分配机制，而非最大化视听分类精度的通用策略。

Abstract: Introduction: Biological systems face anatomical and metabolic constraints, including costly synaptic maintenance and limited connectivity. These constraints favor neural codes that compress behaviorally relevant information into low-redundancy patterns. We test whether an excitatory competitive Hebbian rule can support synaptic resource allocation under such constraints and whether the resulting representations occupy a more favorable cost-performance regime than reference learning rules.
  Methods: Representational cost is quantified using mutual-information-based measures derived from the Variational Information Bottleneck. Experiments use fixed audiovisual embeddings from three audiovisual benchmarks (AVE, Kinetics-Sounds, VGGSound100) to isolate downstream associative plasticity. Hebbian learning is compared with Dense Difference Target Propagation (DDTP) and backpropagation (BP) under matched sparsity and architectural constraints.
  Results: Hebbian learning achieves lower task-information cost (CTI) than sparse BP and DDTP in the main compressed comparisons, while reaching CTI values comparable to shallow BP with nonnegative weights. Rather than uniformly improving classification performance, Hebbian learning shifts the trade-off between task-relevant information and representational cost, yielding lower CTI at comparable functional performance in several settings.
  Discussion: The results indicate a cost-performance trade-off rather than uniform accuracy gains. For a given level of task-relevant information, Hebbian representations retain less input information while preserving functional performance, although accuracy is slightly reduced on some datasets. These findings support interpreting Hebbian learning as a mechanism for synaptic resource allocation rather than as a general strategy for maximizing audiovisual classification accuracy.

</details>


### [127] [Structure of the Circular-Dyadic Convolution Error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15293)
*Ben Fauber,Alireza Moradzadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了用Hadamard变换替代FFT计算循环卷积时产生的代数误差，发现误差具有结构性、可预测性，并受对齐度控制，且渐近地会使输出能量加倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hadamard变换因只涉及实数符号翻转而优于FFT，但替代FFT进行循环卷积时会引入代数误差，作者希望系统地表征这一误差。

Method: 作者通过理论分析给出了三个互补结果：误差精确抵消位置的识别、误差算子的秩分析、以及通过随机滤波器平均得到的闭合形式误差表达式。

Result: 误差在特定输入输出位置恰好抵消；误差算子几乎满秩，零空间仅具有对数维度；期望误差由单一对齐标量控制，可闭式表达；替代误差渐近地使输出能量加倍，除非滤波器属于无误差子空间。

Conclusion: 该替代误差并非杂乱无章，而是结构化的、可预测的，并本质上由滤波器与变换的对齐程度决定。

Abstract: Dyadic and circular convolution can both be computed in $O(N\log N)$ time using the Hadamard transform and the FFT-computed discrete Fourier transform (DFT), respectively. The Hadamard transform is preferable for its real-valued sign flips, yet its substitution for the DFT introduces algebraic error. We present three complementary results that characterize this error. First, we identify exact error cancellation: two input and two output positions are universally error-free, and no reordering of the output can eliminate this error. Second, the error operator is nearly full rank, while its null space has only logarithmic dimension. Third, the expected error is governed by a single alignment scalar, with a closed-form expression obtained by averaging over random filters. In general, the substitution error asymptotically doubles the output energy, except for filters in the universal zero-error subspace, which incur no error. Collectively, these results show that the substitution error is structured, predictable, and governed by alignment.

</details>

Abstract: The scaling hypothesis assumes that increasing model parameters yields emergent reasoning capabilities. This position paper argues that applying this probabilistic paradigm to generic quantum circuit synthesis is a directional error. Unlike natural languages, quantum circuits require strict adherence to mathematical constraints that manifest a significant syntax-semantics gap. Training on unverified quantum programs means that models learn syntax but fail to capture the physical semantics of the Hilbert space. Since the valid subset of circuit designs decays exponentially with the number of qubits, post-hoc filtering is mathematically intractable. We propose a pivot from human-centric copilots to verifier-centric agents. We integrate hierarchical constraints, topological masks, and symbolic proxies directly into generation. Our analysis suggests that scale alone cannot bridge the validity gap. Verification-aware architectures offer a viable path for modular quantum program generation. These considerations point toward generation methods that encode task-specific rules of quantum information, rather than relying on imitation alone.

Abstract: Black-box models limit the adoption of artificial intelligence in medicine due to their lack of interpretability and reproducibility. The method applies supervised $χ^2$-guided statistical binarization to continuous variables, identifying thresholds that maximize association with clinical outcomes within the training data. This transformation allows BNB to operate effectively on continuous medical data without sacrificing its inherent transparency. The approach was evaluated on three benchmark datasets, Pima Indians Diabetes, Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and Heart Failure Prediction, achieving area-under-the-curve (AUC) scores of 0.800 for the Pima analysis, 0.984 for Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and 0.919 for Heart Failure Prediction. In addition to discrimination, probabilistic reliability was assessed using leakage-safe cross-validated calibration analysis including Brier score, calibration intercept/slope, and post-hoc beta calibration, which improved probability calibration across datasets. ### [130] [Regularity-Aware Stochastic MGDA with Adaptive Conflict-Avoidant Update Direction Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15412)
*Chentong Huang,Lisha Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对随机多梯度下降算法（SMG）收敛速度慢的问题，发现其根源在于冲突规避（CA）方向关于雅可比矩阵仅具有1/2-Hölder连续性。作者提出了一种名为MoRe的随机多目标正则性感知方法，在子问题正则时利用CA方向的Lipschitz连续性，否则切换至固定标量化权重。该方法在非凸设定下将收敛率从𝒪̃(T^{-1/4})提升至𝒪̃(T^{-1/2})，并保持了逐迭代的冲突规避保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机多梯度下降方法（SMG）由于小批量采样引入梯度噪声，导致更新方向存在偏差，收敛速度缓慢。作者旨在揭示这一问题的根本原因，并设计一种能有效提升收敛率的随机多目标优化算法。

Method: 本文首先理论分析了CA方向的连续性，证明其仅为1/2-Hölder连续（且最坏情况下不可改进），但在额外正则条件下可提升至Lipschitz连续。基于此，提出MoRe方法：当子问题正则（梯度冲突较大）时，利用Lipschitz连续性进行CA方向更新；否则切换至固定标量化权重（线性标量化更新）。

Result: 在非凸设定下，MoRe方法将SMG的收敛率从𝒪̃(T^{-1/4})提升至𝒪̃(T^{-1/2})，同时建立了逐迭代的冲突规避保证。实验验证了多任务性能的有效性以及收敛行为与理论速率的一致性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了随机多目标优化中收敛慢的根本原因，并通过理论驱动的算法设计显著提升了收敛率，为多目标学习的随机优化提供了新的理论见解和实用方法。

Abstract: Multi-objective learning (MOL) aims to optimize multiple objectives simultaneously. The multi-gradient descent algorithm (MGDA) is a workhorse that iteratively updates along a common descent or conflict-avoidant (CA) direction across objectives. In stochastic settings, however, the vanilla stochastic MGDA method, SMG, lacks a fast convergence rate because mini-batch sampling introduces noise in the gradients. This causes bias in the update direction, which is controlled by the CA direction continuity. In this paper, we show that the CA direction is $1/2$-Holder continuous with respect to the Jacobian matrix, and the exponent $1/2$ cannot be improved in the worst case. This leads to a suboptimal convergence rate for vanilla stochastic MGDA in prior works. Nevertheless, under additional regularity conditions, we show this can be improved to Lipschitz continuity. Based on this insight, we propose a stochastic multi-objective regularity-aware (MoRe) method that exploits the Lipschitz continuity of the CA direction when the subproblem is regular, and switches to a fixed scalarization weight otherwise. Intuitively, the proposed algorithm employs CA direction update when the gradient conflict is large, and linear scalarization update otherwise. Theoretically, our method improves the convergence rate of SMG in the nonconvex setting from $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(T^{-1/4})$ to $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(T^{-1/2})$, where $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(\cdot)$ hides logarithmic factors. Meanwhile, we also establish the per-iterate conflict-avoidance guarantees. Empirically, experiments demonstrate its effectiveness in multi-task performance and verify convergence behavior consistent with the established theoretical rate.

</details>

Abstract: We characterize and compare the inherent interpretability offerings of a standard linear model with a single qubit mixed state model for the task of supervised binary classification. ### [134] [Stochastic Reset Pathfinding: Path-Level Regret for Cascading Bandits over Graph Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15440)
*Guni Sharon,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出随机重置寻路问题（SRP），将其纳入组合级联强盗框架，并提出基于UCB和汤普森采样的Log-Dijkstra元算法，在理论上证明了路径级遗憾界，实验表明PathTS在多数场景表现最佳但存在对抗性失败实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实场景（量子中继器网络、闪电网络支付路由、不可靠网状网络交付）中，代理需在已知图上规划路径，但边的成功概率未知，且执行中任何边失败都会将代理重置回起点，现有算法难以有效处理这种全局重置结构。

Method: 将SRP建模为组合级联强盗问题，证明最优策略是开环的；提出Log-Dijkstra元算法，包括PathUCB（上置信界）和PathTS（汤普森采样）两种实例化；核心理论贡献是路径级遗憾界，通过每条路径的复杂度C(π)（结合前缀和后缀的边可靠性）分解遗憾。

Result: 在量子网络、分层DAG、网格世界、Erdős–Rényi图上进行实验，支持理论分析；PathTS在多数测试算法中取得最佳经验性能；但构造了一个对抗性实例，表明PathTS可能无法收敛，这与组合汤普森采样在乘性奖励问题上的已知指数障碍一致。

Conclusion: 推荐PathTS作为实用默认算法，但需警示其存在对抗性失败实例；路径级遗憾界比边级界在结构化图上更具信息量；未来工作可探索更鲁棒的算法设计。

Abstract: We introduce Stochastic Reset Pathfinding (SRP), an episodic learning problem on a known directed graph with unknown stationary edge success probabilities. In each episode, the agent commits to a source-to-goal path, and any edge failure during execution resets it to the source. SRP captures settings such as entanglement distribution in quantum repeater networks, payment routing on the Lightning Network, and delivery in unreliable mesh networks. We show that the global-reset structure makes the optimal policy open-loop, placing SRP within the combinatorial cascading bandit (CCB) framework. We propose a Log-Dijkstra meta-algorithm with UCB (PathUCB) and Thompson Sampling (PathTS) instantiations. Our main technical result is a path-level regret bound for PathUCB that decomposes regret over suboptimal paths via a per-path complexity C(pi) combining each edge's prefix and suffix reliability. The bound is complementary to the edge-level CCB bound and more informative on structured graphs with polynomially many source-to-goal paths. Experiments on quantum-network, layered-DAG, grid-world, and Erdos-Renyi domains support the theory and show that PathTS typically achieves the best empirical performance among the algorithms tested. We then exhibit an adversarial instance on which PathTS fails to converge, consistent with a known exponential obstruction for combinatorial Thompson Sampling on multiplicative-reward problems. We recommend PathTS as the practical default while cautioning that adversarial instances exist.

Motivation: 美国医疗费用持续高企，COVID-19疫情可能进一步加剧了医疗财务负担，需要量化评估疫情前后人口层面的医疗财务脆弱性变化及其主要影响因素。

Method: 使用2019年和2021年MEPS数据，以家庭医疗自付支出超过收入10%定义为高财务负担；采用加权子组分析获得全国代表性估计；结合逻辑回归（估计调整优势比）和随机森林、梯度提升机（评估预测性能）进行建模，并检验模型在疫情前训练后对疫情后数据的时域泛化能力。

Result: 医疗财务脆弱性与贫困状况、保险覆盖和处方药支出显著相关；2021年弱势群体负担有所加重；但基于疫情前数据训练的模型在疫情后数据上预测性能仅小幅下降，表明核心预测因素相对稳定。

Conclusion: 研究提供了COVID-19期间医疗财务脆弱性的人口层面评估，展示了可解释统计建模与机器学习结合在人口健康研究中的价值，可为未来的健康监测、风险分层和减少医疗财务障碍的政策研究提供支持。

Abstract: The cost of healthcare remains a concern in the United States and may have been influenced by disruptions associated with the COVID-19 pandemic. This study examines healthcare financial vulnerability before and after the pandemic using Medical Expenditure Panel Survey (MEPS) data from 2019 and 2021. High financial burden was defined as out-of-pocket healthcare expenditures exceeding 10% of family income. Survey-weighted subgroup analyses were performed to obtain nationally representative estimates across demographic and socioeconomic groups.
  Descriptive analyses were complemented by interpretable logistic regression and machine learning models. Logistic regression was used to estimate adjusted odds ratios, while random forest and gradient boosting models were used to evaluate predictive performance. Temporal generalization assessed whether models trained on pre-pandemic data remained predictive when applied to post-pandemic observations.
  Financial vulnerability was strongly associated with poverty status, insurance coverage, and prescription drug spending. Subgroup analyses indicated persistent disparities across population groups, with some evidence of increased burden among vulnerable populations in 2021. Despite these differences, models trained on pre-pandemic data exhibited only modest reductions in predictive performance when evaluated on post-pandemic data, suggesting that the principal predictors of healthcare financial vulnerability remained relatively stable over time.
  These findings provide a population-level assessment of healthcare financial vulnerability during the COVID-19 period and demonstrate the value of combining interpretable statistical modeling with machine learning for population health research. The results may support future population health surveillance, risk stratification, and healthcare policy research aimed at reducing financial barriers to care.

### [137] [Relevant and Irrelevant: A Renormalization Group Analysis of Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15449)
*Parviz Haggi-Mani,Irina Rish*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文运用威尔逊重整化群理论，将Transformer的注意力机制视为对MLP残差流不动点的微扰，通过推导不动点偏移公式和四个可检验预测，在合成马尔可夫链上验证了注意力相关性取决于数据生成过程的谱结构：长程相关时注意力是相关算符，驱动表示空间的相变；短程相关时则是不相关算符。第一层注意力头主导了这一转变，且注意力在长程相关时选择性地保留慢变模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望从重整化群的理论视角理解Transformer中注意力机制的本质作用，回答"注意力机制在什么条件下是必要的"这一核心问题，超越简单的架构比较，揭示数据统计特性与注意力有效性之间的深层联系。

Method: 使用Wilson重整化群语言，将注意力机制视为对训练好的MLP残差流不动点的微扰，推导不动点偏移公式，获得四个可检验预测（不动点几何、有效秩分布、层特异性、微扰衰减谱），并在可控相关长度的合成马尔可夫链序列上进行实证验证。

Result: (1)长相关序列中注意力是强相关算符，驱动表示空间的相变，有效秩跃升超过输入维度；(2)短相关序列中注意力不相关，Transformer收敛到与MLP相同的不动点和损失；(3)第一层第一个注意力头贡献了超4倍的表示偏移，主导转变；(4)长相关时注意力选择性保留慢变马尔可夫模式（动态范围5.4倍 vs MLP 1.3倍），短相关时无谱选择性。

Conclusion: 注意力的相关性不是架构固有的属性，而是取决于数据生成过程的谱结构；一阶RG微扰框架能够预测这种差异，为理解Transformer在不同数据条件下的行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Using the language of Wilsonian renormalization group theory (RG), we treat the Transformer's attention mechanism as a perturbation of the trained MLP residual-stack fixed point and ask whether it constitutes a relevant, marginal, or irrelevant operator. We derive a fixed-point shift formula and obtain four testable predictions for the fixed-point geometry, effective rank profile, layer specificity, and perturbation decay spectrum. Testing these on synthetic Markov chain sequences with controlled correlation length, we find: (1) For large chains(long correlation), attention is strongly relevant: it closes a residual loss gap the MLP cannot bridge and drives a phase transition in representation space, with effective rank jumping above input dimensionality at layer 1 and stabilizing at a high-dimensional plateau. (2) For short chains(short correlation), attention is irrelevant: the Transformer converges to the same loss and fixed-point geometry as the MLP, though it contracts perturbations faster. (3) The transition is dominated by the first-layer head (L0H0), which accounts for more than 4 times the representational shift of any subsequent head, consistent with the prediction that the relevant operator acts before the MLP begins integrating out positional variation. (4) Perturbation decay experiments reveal a regime reversal: in the long correlation regime the Transformer selectively preserves slow Markov modes (5.4 times the dynamic range in decay length vs. 1.3 times for the MLP); in the short correlation regime it suppresses all modes faster than the MLP, with no spectral selectivity. Together, these results show that the relevance of attention is not a property of the architecture but of the spectral structure of the data-generating process, and that a first-order RG perturbation framework provides a predictive account of that difference.

</details>


### [138] [Looped Latent Attention: Cross-Loop KV Compression for Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15456)
*James O' Neill,Fergal Reid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出循环潜在注意力(LLA)，一种针对循环、权重共享Transformer的后训练缓存编解码器。通过利用K/V向量在循环维度上的低秩轨迹结构，LLA将紧凑的K/V潜在表示存储起来，仅当注意力需要时才重构循环特定的K/V向量。在同等缓存预算下，逐头LLA优于MLA、跨层共享、KV量化和最终循环重用等方法。在H200上实现21.3倍压缩，将Ouro-1.4B批处理容量从32提升至768序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环权重共享Transformer虽然减少了参数，但解码时仍为每个循环步骤存储独立的K/V缓存，导致缓存开销随循环次数线性增长。作者发现这些缓存具有高度结构化的低秩特性，启发设计专门利用循环维度冗余的压缩方法。

Method: 提出循环潜在注意力(LLA)：1) 默认逐头编解码器压缩循环维度，将K/V映射到低维潜在空间；2) LLA-2D扩展将头维度也折叠进同一潜在表示实现极端压缩；3) 初始化为教师激活的SVD分解，通过KL散度和注意力输出蒸馏进行后训练优化。

Result: 在同等缓存预算下，逐头LLA优于MLA、跨层共享、KV量化等方法。在H200上，以21.3倍压缩将Ouro-1.4B在4k上下文下的批处理容量从32提升至768序列。在长数学推理任务中，学生生成前缀上的策略内精炼将MATH-500从0.43提升至0.66（4倍压缩），并减少无答案生成。

Conclusion: 循环缓存是低秩的，但不能安全地折叠为单一状态。循环轴上的压缩优势在Ouro-2.6B-Thinking和Huginn-3.5B上均有验证，SVD编解码器在32倍压缩下仍保持近乎无损的解码器无关评估性能。

Abstract: Looped, weight-tied Transformers reduce parameters by reusing a block, but decoding still stores a separate K/V cache for every recurrence step. We show that this loop-indexed cache is highly structured. For a fixed token, layer and head, K/V vectors trace a short low-rank trajectory across loops, while the head and layer axes remain much flatter. We introduce Looped Latent Attention (LLA), a post-training cache codec that stores compact K and V latents and reconstructs loop-specific K/V vectors only when attention reads them. The default per-head codec compresses recurrence, while LLA-2D also folds heads into one latent for the extreme-compression regime. The codec is initialized from SVD of teacher activations and refined with KL and attention-output distillation. At matched cache budget, per-head LLA outperforms head-axis MLA, cross-layer sharing, KV quantization and final-loop reuse, showing that the recurrent cache is low-rank but not safely collapsible to a single state. The same axis advantage holds on Ouro-2.6B-Thinking and transfers to Huginn-3.5B, where an SVD codec remains near-lossless to 32x in decoder-independent evaluation. The cache reduction is exact. On one H200, the latent-store path increases measured Ouro-1.4B batch capacity at 4k context from 32 to 768 sequences at 21.3x compression. For long math rollouts, on-policy refinement on student-generated prefixes raises MATH-500 at 4x from 0.43 to 0.66 and reduces no-answer generations.

### [139] [Robust Peak-cost Constrained Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15457)
*Shilpa Mukhopadhyay,Sourav Ganguly,Santosh Mohan Rajkumar,Honghao Wei,Debdipta Goswami,Arnob Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究鲁棒峰值代价约束强化学习（RP-CRL），目标是最大化期望奖励同时控制轨迹中最大代价。发现峰值代价约束MDP可能不存在零对偶间隙，并提出基于积分概率度量的代理优化框架与鲁棒价值估计方法。实验表明该方法在动力学扰动下能有效保障安全并保持高奖励性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CMDP基于期望累积代价，无法捕捉单次大违规带来的灾难性后果。峰值代价约束能更好描述这类安全关键场景，但其对偶性质尚不明确，且存在仿真-真实动力学失配问题。

Method: 1) 理论分析显示峰值代价约束MDP可能不存在零对偶间隙；2) 提出鲁棒优化框架；3) 基于积分概率度量（IPM）开发鲁棒价值估计方法；4) 构建代理优化问题，通过适当超参数选择，使代理解在约束最多违反ε的前提下达到与原问题相同的鲁棒奖励值。

Result: 理论证明了代理优化与原始问题在鲁棒奖励上的等价性及约束有界偏离；实验表明该方法在动力学扰动下有效保障安全，同时保持强奖励性能。

Conclusion: 峰值代价约束MDP与标准CMDP具有本质不同的对偶性质，提出的鲁棒方法能有效处理动力学不确定下的安全约束问题。

Abstract: We study robust peak-cost constrained reinforcement learning (RP-CRL), where the objective is to maximize expected reward while controlling the maximum cost encountered along a trajectory. This setting is motivated by safety-critical applications in which a single large violation can be catastrophic and therefore cannot be adequately captured by the standard CMDP framework based on expected cumulative cost. Existing reachability-constrained RL methods adopt Lagrangian-based approaches, yet the underlying duality properties of peak-cost constrained MDPs remain unclear. We show that, unlike standard CMDPs, peak-cost constrained MDPs may not admit zero duality gap. We further consider a robust formulation to address simulator-to-real-world mismatch in the transition dynamics. To solve this problem, we develop a surrogate optimization framework and a robust value estimation method based on integral probability metrics. We prove that, with appropriate hyperparameter choices, the surrogate solution attains the same robust reward value as the original problem while violating the constraint by at most epsilon. Experiments show that the proposed method effectively enforces safety under dynamics perturbations while retaining strong reward performance.

### [140] [ADS-C: Antidistillation Sampling for Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15467)
*Khawaja Abaid Ullah,Mohammad Javad Khojasteh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ADS-C，一种针对分类任务的抗蒸馏防御方法。该方法通过输入相关的梯度方向扰动保护教师模型输出概率，在保证top-1预测不变（即教师准确率完全无损）的前提下，显著降低蒸馏学生模型的性能。实验表明在CIFAR-100、CIFAR-10和Tiny-ImageNet上，学生准确率分别下降17.4、29.6和13.3个百分点，而教师准确率完全不受影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识蒸馏可以通过查询教师模型预测接口训练替代模型，严重威胁专有分类器的知识产权。现有针对大语言模型的抗蒸馏采样方法尚未迁移到分类任务，且直接迁移存在局限性——由于分类器过度自信，防御存在"惰性窗口"，超过阈值后反而损害教师模型更严重。因此需要一种零代价的分类任务抗蒸馏防御方法。

Method: ADS-C方法：(1) 对教师模型输出的概率分布施加输入相关的梯度方向扰动；(2) 通过闭式解计算每个样本的置信度边界，在该边界内保证top-1预测不变；(3) 温度缩放可闭式调节过渡阈值。核心创新在于闭式逐样本边界约束，使得教师准确率完全不变的同时，扰动足以破坏蒸馏效果。

Result: 在CIFAR-100（学生降17.4pp）、CIFAR-10（降29.6pp）和Tiny-ImageNet（降13.3pp）上，学生模型性能显著下降，而教师准确率完全不变。相比之下，未经修改的防御要达到同等学生性能下降，需牺牲教师27.5、32.9和22.2个百分点的准确率。对硬标签攻击者完全无效，软标签训练的学生准确率比仅用标签的基线还低29.7个百分点。

Conclusion: ADS-C是首个教师准确率零损失（utility cost exactly zero）的分类抗蒸馏防御方法。它不仅消除了蒸馏的激励，还将其反转——使用防御后的软概率训练学生还不如直接使用硬标签。实验覆盖多个数据集，证实了方法的有效性和理论分析的正确性。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation enables an adversary to replicate a proprietary classifier by querying its prediction interface and training a surrogate on the returned probability vectors. Antidistillation sampling, proposed for large language models, counters this threat with an input-dependent, gradient-directed perturbation of the served distribution; its transfer to classification has not been studied. Adapting the defense to classification, we show its behavior is governed by the distribution of the teacher's per-input confidence margins. Because well-trained classifiers are severely overconfident, the direct transfer exhibits an inert window: below a closed-form-predictable threshold, it affects neither attacker nor defender; beyond it, the defense undergoes a phase transition and degrades the teacher faster than the attacker's student. Temperature softening rescales the transition in closed form, and every temperature configuration lies on the same unfavorable trade-off curve. Our method, ADS-C, composes the perturbation under a closed-form, per-input margin budget that provably preserves every served top-1 prediction, so the defended teacher's accuracy equals the undefended teacher's identically. Under this guarantee the distilled student still loses 17.4 percentage points on CIFAR-100, 29.6 on CIFAR-10, and 13.3 on Tiny-ImageNet; matching this degradation with the unmodified defense costs 27.5, 32.9, and 22.2 points of teacher accuracy. Because served labels are unchanged, a hard-label attacker gains nothing, while the defended soft output trains a student up to 29.7 points below that floor: the incentive to distill served probabilities is not merely removed but reversed. To our knowledge, ADS-C is the first antidistillation defense for classification whose utility cost is exactly zero.

</details>

Abstract: Sleep apnea diagnosis via polysomnography remains resource intensive and relies on time consuming manual data analysis and scoring. Recent work has demonstrated that central nervous system effects of sleep apnea events can be detected through electroencephalogram (EEG) signals. However, most work uses a single feature type on various datasets combined with different classification algorithms. In this work, we present a comprehensive comparison of deep learning architectures and feature representations for automated sleep apnea detection from multichannel EEG on a single dataset of pediatric subjects. We evaluate Vision Transformers and Graph Attention Networks across distinct signal representations: raw temporal signals, short-time Fourier transform spectrograms, coherence based graphs, and two topological data analysis (TDA) derived features. Using age and sex matching of our train and test sets, we train on 2410 pediatric subjects and test on 575 pediatric subjects. We achieve a best test AUC of 0.750 using a vision transformer based model trained on TDA features. Stratified analysis across patient demographics (age, sex, AHI severity) and sleep stages (N1, N2, N3, REM) reveals significant performance variation. Our results demonstrate the feasibility of EEG based automated OSA screening while highlighting essential challenges for clinical deployment.

### [142] [Inpainting Insights: Elevating Visual XAI with Photorealistic Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15482)
*Josef Lindl,Mariana Chaves,Damien Garreau*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对基于扰动的XAI方法中生成不真实样本的问题，提出用生成式图像修复技术改进LIME，产生更符合数据分布的光照真实扰动，提升解释质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 生成的扰动样本具有光照真实感，更贴合原始数据分布，提升了解释质量。

Abstract: The increasing complexity of state-of-the-art machine learning models has made their behavior progressively harder to interpret, spurring rapid advancements in the field of eXplainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI). Among many methods proposed, perturbation-based approaches play a major role. By systematically altering (perturbing) input features, these approaches measure the impact on the model's predictions. For image data, traditional perturbation techniques, often involve replacing pixel values e.g., with a pre-defined color. However, such approaches, but also more refined deterministic techniques, generate unrealistic out-of-distribution samples and often leave visible artifacts, which can mislead the model and compromise explanation quality. In this work, we adjust LIME, a widely used perturbation-based method, to demonstrate how generative inpainting can improve perturbation-based explanations for images. We achieve photorealistic perturbed samples that align better with the original data distribution and enhance explanation quality.

### [143] [Diffusion models recover accurate mixture weights despite score function insensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15485)
*Andrew Dennehy,Ramchandran Muthukumar,Rebecca Willett,Nisha Chandramoorthy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出扩散分数敏感性指数（DSSI）解决了分数生成模型中的一个悖论：模型虽然能覆盖所有模态，但可能无法正确学习模态间的混合权重。研究表明，DSM损失与混合权重估计误差之间存在理论联系，并证明噪声调度策略会影响敏感性，进而影响权重的恢复精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数生成模型虽能覆盖多模态分布的所有模态，却常出现模态振幅（即混合权重）估计不准的反常现象。作者旨在解释这一悖论，并建立DSM损失与混合权重估计误差之间的理论关联。

Method: 提出扩散分数敏感性指数（DSSI），定义为DSM损失相对于参数变化的变分；理论上证明了高斯混合下权重估计误差与DSM损失同阶；通过实验验证噪声调度对敏感性的影响以及敏感性对权重恢复效果的预测能力。

Result: 证明了即使目标分数对混合权重不敏感，中间噪声水平的分数仍能提供关于权重的信息；DSSI决定了目标分布参数从生成样本中估计的精度；噪声调度的选择可降低扩散敏感性，从而影响模态放大效应。

Conclusion: DSSI框架不仅适用于混合权重，还适用于目标分布的任何定性参数的恢复；合理选择噪声调度是缓解扩散模型模态放大问题的关键。

Abstract: Score-based generative models exhibit a puzzling behavior: they often appear to cover all modes of a target multimodal distribution and yet may fail to learn the correct relative mode amplitudes, which can be interpreted as mixture weights. We resolve this apparent paradox by relating the diffusion score matching (DSM) loss to the error in estimating mixture weights from generated samples. We show that, even when the target score is insensitive to mixture weights, generated samples can recover the weights accurately if the scores at intermediate noise levels are informative about the weights. Accordingly, we define the diffusion score sensitivity index (DSSI) as the variation in the DSM loss relative to changes in a parameter. We then show that the DSSI governs the accuracy with which the parameter of the target distribution can be estimated from generated samples. For Gaussian mixtures in arbitrary dimensions, we prove that the mixture weight estimation errors are on the same order as the DSM loss under mild conditions. Empirically, we show the emergence of sensitivity during the noising process of benchmark data distributions under typical noise schedules, and that these sensitivity values predict how well a well-trained model recovers mixture weights. Furthermore, we show that the choice of noise schedule can reduce diffusion sensitivity, leading to mode amplification. Although we focus on mixture weights, the proposed sensitivity framework governs the recovery of any qualitative parameter of the target distribution.

Resource demand is predicted using lightweight MLP, LSTM, and CNN models. Their outputs are combined through a performance-weighted probabilistic ensemble inspired by Bayesian model averaging. The controller further incorporates cold-start awareness and cost comparison to select among scale-up, scale-down, and hold actions. Experiments using real workload traces show that supervised forecasting substantially outperforms unsupervised clustering for autoscaling decision generation. The proposed ensemble achieves 99.88 percent prediction accuracy and reduces prediction error compared with representative hybrid forecasting methods. Evaluations across multiple cloud pricing models also demonstrate consistent infrastructure cost reductions while maintaining performance targets. The results show that combining dependency analysis, multi-expert forecasting, and cost-aware control provides a robust and practical solution for serverless autoscaling.
